TITLE      -Fission cross-section measurement on U-235.-          2012900100009 
FACILITY   (LINAC,2ZZZGEL)    CBNM electron linear accelerator.   2012900100010 
            Characteristics of the simultaneous measurements with 2012900100011 
            two detectors for 3 runs given in table 1 (p.217)     2012900100012 
            of J.Nucl.En.,vol 22.                                 2012900100013 
INC-SOURCE (PHOTO).Photo-neutrons from a mercury cooled natural   2012900100014 
            uranium target slowed down by a 2.8 cm thick 20*20 cm22012900100015 
            polyethylene sheet.                                   2012900100016 
INC-SPECT  .The neutron spectrum was proportional to En**(-0.887) 2012900100017 
SAMPLE     .Flight path A (neutr)    *  flight path B (fission)   2012900100018 
            -------------------------*----------------------------2012900100019 
           .Thickness,  a disk of    *  800 microgr/cm2/electrode 2012900100020 
            below 41 eV   above 41 eV*  below 41 eV   above 41 eV 2012900100021

           .Metallic                 * uran-uranyl acetate        2012900100023 
           .Isotopic composition in per-cent,                     2012900100024

METHOD     (TOF  )    time of flight, flight path = 60.58 m.      2012900100030 
           .Two flight paths are used simultaneously forming an   2012900100031 
            angle of -9 and +9 degrees with the axis perpendicular2012900100032 
            to the moderator surface.                             2012900100033 
           .Flight path A has 3 collimators, at the target room,  2012900100034 
            at the 30 m. Station and at the detector station at   2012900100035 
            60 m. The detector is a fission neutron detector.     2012900100036 
           .Flight path B has 2 collimators, at the target room,  2012900100037 
            and in the detector station at 60 m. The detector is  2012900100038 
            a shielded ionization chamber.                        2012900100039 
DETECTOR   (SCIN )    4 liquid scintillation chambers forming a   2012900100040 
            hollow cylinder with outer diam.38 cm, outer length   2012900100041 
            38 cm, inner diam.16 cm,inner length 16 cm.           2012900100042 
           .Sample in the middle of the cylinder.                 2012900100043 
           .Filled with NE213 liquid scintillator.                2012900100044 
           .Each chamber is viewed by a 58 AVP photomultiplier,   2012900100045 
            via a pulse shape gamma discriminator pair-wise linked2012900100046 
            to six two-input coincidence circuits giving a stop   2012900100047 
            signal to the time-of-flight analyzer via an 'or' gate2012900100048 
           .This detector detects fission neutrons on             2012900100049 
            flight path A.                                        2012900100050 
           (IOCH) .Six (above 41 eV eight) argon (+5% C-O(2))     2012900100051 
            filled (450 torr) ionization chambers,                2012900100052 
           .Electrodes 26 cm diameter 35 mm thick aluminium foils 2012900100053 
            on 4 mm distance at 500 volts.                        2012900100054 
           .Sample on one of the electrodes.                      2012900100055 
           .In aluminium box with 0.6 mm thick windows.           2012900100056 
           .Discriminated against alpha particles up to 20 MeV    2012900100057 
           .Total time resolution 100 nanosec FWHM.               2012900100058 
           .This detector detects fission fragments on            2012900100059 
            flight path B.                                        2012900100060 
           (BF3) .For neutron flux measurements a bank of BF3-    2012900100061 
            counters placed 1 m behind the fission detectors      2012900100062 
           .Shielded against low energy background neutrons by    2012900100063 
            0.7 mm Cd.                                            2012900100064 
MONITOR    (92-U-235(N,F),,ARE)  integral(sigma(E)*dE) between    2012900100065 
            8 and 10 eV (S.F.Shore, V.L.Sailor, Phys.Rev.,        2012900100066 
            112(1958)191) for the lower energy run.               2012900100067 
           .The Shore data are normalized to a 2200 m/sec         2012900100068 
            cross-section of 582 barn.                            2012900100069 
           .Higher energy runs have been normalized via the       2012900100070 
            integral over the overlap region.                     2012900100071 
REL-REF    (R,12418004,S.F.Shore+,J,PR,112,191,1958)              2012900100072 
CORRECTION .Corrected for background by black resonance technique.2012900100073 
           .No correction for resolution and Doppler effects      2012900100074
